Serve.</p>\\r\\n\\r\\n<p>6.&nbsp; Stir Fry</p>\\r\\n\\r\\n<p>Make a stir-fry: Toss chopped leftover veg in a pan with soy sauce or sauce of choice.</p>\\r\\n\\r\\n<p>7.&nbsp; Quick Curry</p>\\r\\n\\r\\n<p>For a quick curry: fry onion and garlic, then add coconut milk and curry paste and cubed leftover vegies.&nbsp; Serve with some steamed rice.</p>\\r\\n\\r\\n<p>8.&nbsp; Bubble and squeak</p>\\r\\n\\r\\n<p>For a quick side dish, mash 3 cups of chopped leftover roasted vegetables. Whisk 2 eggs then add 1/4 cup of flour and 1 tablespoon of water. Combine with mashed vegetables. Mould into patties. Spray with oil. Pan-fry each side on medium heat until crisp and golden.</p>\\r\\n\\r\\n<p>9.&nbsp; Stew</p>\\r\\n\\r\\n<p>Use up leftover vegetables by simply adding them to a stew. Cook meat as you normally would, then add stock and chopped leftover vegies until heated through.</p>\\r\\n\\r\\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\\r\\n\\r\\n<p>Ingredients vary weekly based on recipe requirements.</p>\\r\\n\\r\\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\\r\\n\\r\\n<table border=\\\"0\\\" cellpadding=\\\"0\\\" cellspacing=\\\"0\\\" style=\\\"width:319px\\\">\\r\\n\\t<tbody>\\r\\n\\t\\t<tr>\\r\\n\\t\\t\\t<td
